Run Summary

Target:
x^2 + 2xy + y^2
Iterations:
500
Best leaf matches target:
Yes
Best leaf mean value:
1.000
Best leaf visits:
17
Best leaf polynomial:
x^2 + 2xy + y^2
The tree policy relies on the Upper Confidence Bound for Trees (UCT): UCT = Q + c * sqrt(ln(N_parent) / N_child), where Q is the mean value of a child, c is the exploration constant, and N counts visits. Each iteration follows four phases: selection via UCT, expansion of a new action, a random rollout (simulation), and value backpropagation.
